<h1 class="header"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="name">Michael Jackson</span>
<span>(I)</span>
<span>(1958–2009)</span>
</h1>
<div class="infobar" id="name-job-categories">
<a href="#soundtrack" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Soundtrack</span></a> <span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="#actor" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Actor</span></a> <span class="ghost">|</span>
<a href="#producer" onclick="nameJobCategoriesClickHandler(this)"> <span class="itemprop" itemprop="jobTitle">
Producer</span></a>
</div>
<hr/>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-bio-text">
<div class="name-trivia-bio-text">
<div class="inline" itemprop="description">
Michael Joseph Jackson was born in Gary, Indiana on August 29, 1958, and entertained audiences nearly his entire life. His father, <a href="/name/nm1129499?ref_=nm_ov_bio_lk1">Joe Jackson</a>, had been a guitarist, but was forced to give up his musical ambitions following his marriage to <a href="/name/nm1808277?ref_=nm_ov_bio_lk2">Katherine Jackson</a> (née Katherine Esther Scruse). Together, they prodded their growing family's musical ...            <span class="see-more inline nobr-only">
<a href="/name/nm0001391/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bio_sm">See full bio</a> »
            </span>
</div> </div>
</div>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-born-info">
<h4 class="inline">Born:</h4>
<a href="/name/nm0001391/bio?ref_=nm_ov_bth_nm"> Michael Joseph Jackson
</a> <br/>
<time datetime="1958-8-29" itemprop="birthDate">
<a href="/search/name?birth_monthday=8-29&amp;refine=birth_monthday&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_monthday">August 29</a>, 
     
<a href="/search/name?birth_year=1958&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_year">1958</a>
</time>
            in
            <a href="/search/name?birth_place=Gary%2C+Indiana%2C+USA&amp;ref_=nm_ov_bth_place">Gary, Indiana, USA</a>
</div>
<div class="txt-block" id="name-death-info">
<h4 class="inline">Died:</h4>
<time datetime="2009-6-25" itemprop="deathDate">
<a href="/search/name?death_monthday=6-25&amp;refine=death_monthday&amp;ref_=nm_ov_dth_monthday">June 25</a>, 
     
<a href="/search/name?death_date=2009&amp;ref_=nm_ov_dth_year">2009</a>
</time>
         (age 50) 
         in <a href="/search/name?death_place=Holmby+Hills%2C+Los+Angeles%2C+California%2C+USA&amp;ref_=nm_ov_dth_place">Holmby Hills, Los Angeles, California, USA</a>
</div>
</td>
<tr>
<td id="overview-middle">
</td>
</tr>
</tr></tbody>
</table>
